msg:The good things about this hotel are that the staff are friendly and kind, the rooms are spacious, and the beds are comfortable. 

Unfortunately, the standard of cleaning is extremely poor for a hotel of this price range. In our room, I had to clean food or drink spills left by previous guests off the bedside tables before using them. The carpet in the room and in the corridors had many stains. The bathroom sink was partly blocked and drained slowly, there was dirt in the corners of the bathroom, and it smelled bad in the toilet. There was dust or smoke stains on the ceiling around the air conditioner. Most disgusting of all, I found a large nail clipping from a previous guest on the floor beside the bed.

Don‚Äôt be fooled by the fancy-looking decorations and good reviews, maybe it was better in the past, but the management of this hotel sets low standards for cleaning and maintenance now. There are many other good hotels in Chengdu for the same price, I strongly suggest you choose another one.

I strongly recommend ex-pats to experience this hotel, which offers service like none of the big chain hotels do. From the moment I walked through the entrance on my first day, to leaving on the last - every interaction was exceptional! Basil, the Deputy Manager was incredible - no question or request was too much, and his attention to detail and attentive service made my stay in the hotel and in Chengdu amazing. He helped me to arrange everything from laundry to tickets to the Sichuan opera, and  genuinely cared about my stay with Wanda Reign. Even after I left he kept kept touch to ensure my further travel plans worked out. The decor of the hotel was truly beautiful, the most wonderful chandeliers and attention to detail everywhere was exceptional. The cleaning team did a phenomenal job, and the room was made up twice a day - with lovely touches such as little personalised notes and presents! I am a stickler for cleaning and genuinely I could not fault any area of cleanliness in this hotel. The room was incredibly well equipped, with a deep soak bath, excellent range of drinks / coffee machine and a super comfy bed! Electric curtains and smart technology using an IPAD to control everything was really efficient. I also have to comment on the wall paper in the room - it was beautiful! The food selection offered and amazing aray of Eastern and Western food to meet all tastes, and the lobby lounge served excellent coffee, afternoon tea, wine and cocktails - with exceptional service and lovely view! The service in the bar was incredible - Eudora was particularly helpful and welcoming. The equipment in the gym was high quality and offered a range of cardio and weight machines, and the pool was a relaxing place to unwind. I really didn't want to leave this hotel, and I will absolutely use this hotel and this brand again in the near future. I can't recommend it highly enough! The remote control and seat surface are very worn, and there is no desire to use it. Secondly, the refrigeration effect of the minibar is very weak. Cold drinks and fruits cannot meet the refrigeration effect below 15 degrees if left for a whole day and cannot be adjusted. The toilet seat heating and flushing functions are malfunctioning. Finally, the shower head on the top of the shower leaked. The small shower head turned on the hot water and the big shower head dripped cold water. It was very uncomfortable and I didn't want to wash my hair but my hair got wet.
The service attitude is very obvious. When checking in, the concierge and service staff helped carry the luggage from the car to the room. When checking out, I said in the lobby that I wanted to store the luggage and directly replied that I would take it to the front desk on the first floor. The same goes for taxis. Non-luxury cars are not allowed to park in front of the hotel. Guests can get on the car they requested by themselves. It is very embarrassing to be pointed by the concierge to park farther away when there is no car in front of the hotel. . Although there is a butler plus WeChat, the functionality is better than nothing. There is no first-round courtesy service in the minibar. Temporary check-out is not until 1 pm at most. No matter how we communicate, we cannot coordinate. The service is very blunt. I wonder if the hotel has dropped its star rating.
The public areas of the hotel are well decorated, but what guests are ultimately willing to pay for is the facilities in the room and the hotel's services, not the rigid wall decorations and floor tiles!
To be honest [I would prefer to choose many high-altitude hotels near Taikoo Li at the same price], the services and facilities are not good enough. Wanda Ruihua will never choose it again in the future.
